<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />
</span></span></p>	                               <style type='text/css'>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />
</span></span></p>	                               <style type='text/css'>

</style>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />

<script type='text/javascript'>
function openAWindow( pageToLoad, winName, width, height, center)
{
    xposition=0; yposition=0;
    if ((parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 4 ) && (center)){
        xposition = (screen.width - width) / 2;
        yposition = (screen.height - height) / 2;
    }
	
	//0 => no
	//1 => yes
    var args = "";
    	args += "width=" + width + "," + "height=" + height + ","
		+ "location=0,"
		+ "menubar=0,"
		+ "resizable=0,"
		+ "scrollbars=0,"
		+ "statusbar=false,dependent,alwaysraised,"
		+ "status=false,"
		+ "titlebar=no,"
		+ "toolbar=0,"
		+ "hotkeys=0,"
		+ "screenx=" + xposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "screeny=" + yposition + ","  //NN Only
		+ "left=" + xposition + ","     //IE Only
		+ "top=" + yposition;           //IE Only
		//fullscreen=yes, add for full screen
    	var dmcaWin = window.open(pageToLoad,winName,args );
    	dmcaWin.focus();
    //window.showModalDialog(pageToLoad,"","dialogWidth:650px;dialogHeight:500px");
}
</script>

<p>&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-size: 1.4em;"><span style="font-family: Arial;">Community Housing Accommodations Listing Service (ALS)  </span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">Queen's does not endorse or warrant the quality of the rental units provided through this listing service</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(187, 0, 0);">. </span></span></span><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">It is a tool to help students in need of rental accommodation connect with landlords who have rental properties available. <br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Some landlords have special agreements with the University whereby they have had a specific unit inspected by an independent third party within the last 12 months to certify that the unit met minimum property standards per City of Kingston By-Law 2005-100. These units are identified by the tri colour flag in the summary and detail information:<br />
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 0.8em;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">We strongly encourage students to become informed consumers by reading available materials, asking questions, etc.It is the student's responsibility to ensure that prospective accommodation is appropriate, suitable and safe.<br />
</span></span></p>	                               <style type='text/css'>
